{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{pixfmt_8h_a3da0bf691418bc22c4bcbe6583ad589a}{A\+V\+Color\+Range}}}

Visual content value range.

These values are based on definitions that can be found in multiple specifications, such as I\+T\+U-\/T B\+T.\+709 (3.\+4 -\/ Quantization of R\+GB, luminance and colour-\/difference signals), I\+T\+U-\/T B\+T.\+2020 (\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_table}{Table}} 5 -\/ Digital Representation) as well as I\+T\+U-\/T B\+T.\+2100 (\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_table}{Table}} 9 -\/ Digital 10-\/ and 12-\/bit integer representation). At the time of writing, the B\+T.\+2100 one is recommended, as it also defines the full range representation.

Common definitions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item For R\+GB and luminance planes such as Y in Y\+Cb\+Cr and I in I\+Ct\+Cp, \textquotesingle{}E\textquotesingle{} is the original value in range of 0.\+0 to 1.\+0.
\item For chrominance planes such as Cb,Cr and Ct,Cp, \textquotesingle{}E\textquotesingle{} is the original value in range of -\/0.\+5 to 0.\+5.
\item \textquotesingle{}n\textquotesingle{} is the output bit depth.
\item For additional definitions such as rounding and clipping to valid n bit unsigned integer range, please refer to B\+T.\+2100 (\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_table}{Table}} 9). 
\end{DoxyItemize}\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AVCOL\_RANGE\_UNSPECIFIED@{AVCOL\_RANGE\_UNSPECIFIED}!pixfmt.h@{pixfmt.h}}\index{pixfmt.h@{pixfmt.h}!AVCOL\_RANGE\_UNSPECIFIED@{AVCOL\_RANGE\_UNSPECIFIED}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{pixfmt_8h_a3da0bf691418bc22c4bcbe6583ad589aaa374becbc2b5ee0bc1886048d151ea3e}\label{pixfmt_8h_a3da0bf691418bc22c4bcbe6583ad589aaa374becbc2b5ee0bc1886048d151ea3e}} 
A\+V\+C\+O\+L\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+G\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+S\+P\+E\+C\+I\+F\+I\+ED&\\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AVCOL\_RANGE\_MPEG@{AVCOL\_RANGE\_MPEG}!pixfmt.h@{pixfmt.h}}\index{pixfmt.h@{pixfmt.h}!AVCOL\_RANGE\_MPEG@{AVCOL\_RANGE\_MPEG}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{pixfmt_8h_a3da0bf691418bc22c4bcbe6583ad589aa00fd8f9315f17e8a0eda86c87da63c0b}\label{pixfmt_8h_a3da0bf691418bc22c4bcbe6583ad589aa00fd8f9315f17e8a0eda86c87da63c0b}} 
A\+V\+C\+O\+L\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+G\+E\+\_\+\+M\+P\+EG&Narrow or limited range content.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item For luminance planes\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}(219 * E + 16) * 2^(n-8)
\end{DoxyVerb}


F.\+ex. the range of 16-\/235 for 8 bits
\item For chrominance planes\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}(224 * E + 128) * 2^(n-8)
\end{DoxyVerb}


F.\+ex. the range of 16-\/240 for 8 bits 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AVCOL\_RANGE\_JPEG@{AVCOL\_RANGE\_JPEG}!pixfmt.h@{pixfmt.h}}\index{pixfmt.h@{pixfmt.h}!AVCOL\_RANGE\_JPEG@{AVCOL\_RANGE\_JPEG}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{pixfmt_8h_a3da0bf691418bc22c4bcbe6583ad589aafce51dfb8b012df5cbbf59918c410f29}\label{pixfmt_8h_a3da0bf691418bc22c4bcbe6583ad589aafce51dfb8b012df5cbbf59918c410f29}} 
A\+V\+C\+O\+L\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+G\+E\+\_\+\+J\+P\+EG&Full range content.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item For R\+GB and luminance planes\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}(2^n - 1) * E
\end{DoxyVerb}


F.\+ex. the range of 0-\/255 for 8 bits
\item For chrominance planes\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}(2^n - 1) * E + 2^(n - 1)
\end{DoxyVerb}


F.\+ex. the range of 1-\/255 for 8 bits 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AVCOL\_RANGE\_NB@{AVCOL\_RANGE\_NB}!pixfmt.h@{pixfmt.h}}\index{pixfmt.h@{pixfmt.h}!AVCOL\_RANGE\_NB@{AVCOL\_RANGE\_NB}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{pixfmt_8h_a3da0bf691418bc22c4bcbe6583ad589aab720c777af1784c9197b3d844de36485}\label{pixfmt_8h_a3da0bf691418bc22c4bcbe6583ad589aab720c777af1784c9197b3d844de36485}}

Definition at line 483 of file pixfmt.\+h.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{pixfmt_8h_a9a8e335cf3be472042bc9f0cf80cd4c5}\label{pixfmt_8h_a9a8e335cf3be472042bc9f0cf80cd4c5}} 
\index{pixfmt.h@{pixfmt.h}!AVPixelFormat@{AVPixelFormat}}
\index{AVPixelFormat@{AVPixelFormat}!pixfmt.h@{pixfmt.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AVPixelFormat}{AVPixelFormat}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{pixfmt_8h_a9a8e335cf3be472042bc9f0cf80cd4c5}{A\+V\+Pixel\+Format}}}

Pixel format.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
A\+V\+\_\+\+P\+I\+X\+\_\+\+F\+M\+T\+\_\+\+R\+G\+B32 is handled in an endian-\/specific manner. An R\+G\+BA color is put together as\+: (A $<$$<$ 24) $\vert$ (R $<$$<$ 16) $\vert$ (G $<$$<$ 8) $\vert$ B This is stored as B\+G\+RA on little-\/endian C\+PU architectures and A\+R\+GB on big-\/endian C\+P\+Us.

If the resolution is not a multiple of the chroma subsampling factor then the chroma plane resolution must be rounded up.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
When the pixel format is palettized R\+G\+B32 (A\+V\+\_\+\+P\+I\+X\+\_\+\+F\+M\+T\+\_\+\+P\+A\+L8), the palettized image data is stored in \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_frame_a1d0f65014a8d1bf78cec8cbed2304992}{A\+V\+Frame.\+data}}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}. The palette is transported in \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_frame_a1d0f65014a8d1bf78cec8cbed2304992}{A\+V\+Frame.\+data}}\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}, is 1024 bytes long (256 4-\/byte entries) and is formatted the same as in A\+V\+\_\+\+P\+I\+X\+\_\+\+F\+M\+T\+\_\+\+R\+G\+B32 described above (i.\+e., it is also endian-\/specific). Note also that the individual R\+G\+B32 palette components stored in \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_frame_a1d0f65014a8d1bf78cec8cbed2304992}{A\+V\+Frame.\+data}}\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} should be in the range 0..255. This is important as many custom P\+A\+L8 video codecs that were designed to run on the I\+BM V\+GA graphics adapter use 6-\/bit palette components.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For all the 8 bits per pixel formats, an R\+G\+B32 palette is in data\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} like for pal8. This palette is filled in automatically by the function allocating the picture. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

Notice that each 9/10 bits sample is stored in 16 bits with extra padding. If you want to support multiple bit depths, then using A\+V\+\_\+\+P\+I\+X\+\_\+\+F\+M\+T\+\_\+\+Y\+U\+V420\+P16$\ast$ with the bpp stored separately is better. \\

This is preferred over the legacy A\+V\+\_\+\+P\+I\+X\+\_\+\+F\+M\+T\+\_\+\+D3\+D11\+V\+A\+\_\+\+V\+LD. The new D3\+D11 hwaccel A\+PI and filtering support A\+V\+\_\+\+P\+I\+X\+\_\+\+F\+M\+T\+\_\+\+D3\+D11 only.

data\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} contains a I\+D3\+D11\+Texture2D pointer, and data\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} contains the texture array index of the frame as intptr\+\_\+t if the I\+D3\+D11\+Texture2D is an array texture (or always 0 if it\textquotesingle{}s a normal texture). \\
